s.tl('TnT', 'o', 'TnT');
s.linkTrackVars = ltv;
s.linkTrackEvents = lte;
}
</script></div><script type="text/javascript">var waitFor = function (condition, retryTime, maxRetries, success, failure) {

    failure = failure || function () {};
    var retried = 0;
    var timer = null;

    var waitForImpl = function () {
        if (condition()) {
            window.clearTimeout(timer);
            success();
        } else if (retried &gt; maxRetries) {
            window.clearTimeout(timer);
            failure();
        } else {
            retried++;
            timer = window.setTimeout(waitForImpl, retryTime);
        }
    };

    waitForImpl();
};</script><script type="text/javascript" async="" src="//sports2.staticcache.org/whassets/_cdn/js/sportsbook.js?9ad31748b0c5930ecfa59510fb03ac50"></script><div id="main-off-canvas" class="off-canvas if (window.top !== window.self) {
    window.top.location = window.self.location;
}
// End SAA-5

var waitFor = function (condition, retryTime, maxRetries, success, failure) {

    failure = failure || function () {};

    var retried = 0;
    var timer = null;

    var waitForImpl = function () {
        if (condition()) {
            window.clearTimeout(timer);
            success();
        } else if (retried &gt; maxRetries) {
            window.clearTimeout(timer);
            failure();
        } else {
            retried++;
            timer = window.setTimeout(waitForImpl, retryTime);
        }
    };

    waitForImpl();
};

var appendScriptTag = function(src, async) {

    var s = document.createElement( 'script' );
    s.setAttribute( 'src', src );
    if (async) {

        s.setAttribute("async", "");
    }
    document.body.appendChild( s );
}</script><script async="" src="//sports.staticcache.org/whassets/_cdn/js/misc.js?39d7a1b8949868f8f2f1f41a6fa330d8"></script><script type="text/javascript">var mainBSApi = '//trans.staticcache.org/ob/static_versioned/api/sportsbook/latest/js/minified/OB_SportBook_API_PMT.js';
    waitFor(function () {
        return (window.$);
    }, 50, 300, function () {
